<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526990"></a><a name="N101B1"></a><a name="lsr"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526990;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.14</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526990;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">lsr</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -lsr &lt;args&gt;</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><br></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">ls</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">命令的递归版本。类似于</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">Unix</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中的</span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">ls -R</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526991"></a><a name="N101C4"></a><a name="mkdir"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526991;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.15</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526991;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">mkdir</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mkdir &lt;paths&gt;</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">接受路径指定的</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">uri</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">作为参数，创建这些目录。其行为类似于</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">Unix</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">的</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">mkdir -p</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">，它会创建路径中的各级父目录。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">示例：</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mkdir /user/hadoop/dir1 /user/hadoop/dir2</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mkdir hdfs://host1:port1/user/hadoop/dir hdfs://host2:port2/user/hadoop/dir</span></span></span><span style="color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">返回值：</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">成功返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">0</span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，失败返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">-1</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';">。</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526992"></a><a name="N101F1"></a><a name="movefromLocal"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526992;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.16</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526992;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">movefromLocal</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">dfs -moveFromLocal &lt;src&gt; &lt;dst&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">输出一个</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">”not implemented“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">信息。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526993"></a><a name="N10201"></a><a name="mv"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526993;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.17</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526993;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">mv</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mv URI [URI …] &lt;dest&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">将文件从源路径移动到目标路径。这个命令允许有多个源路径，此时目标路径必须是一个目录。不允许在不同的文件系统间移动文件。不支持文件夹重命令。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">示例：</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mv /user/hadoop/file1 /user/hadoop/file2</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -mv hdfs://host:port/file1 hdfs://host:port/file2 hdfs://host:port/file3 hdfs://host:port/dir1</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">返回值：</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">成功返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">0</span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，失败返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">-1</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';">。</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526994"></a><a name="N1022B"></a><a name="put"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526994;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.18</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526994;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">put</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -put &lt;localsrc&gt; ... &lt;dst&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">从本地文件系统中复制单个或多个源路径到目标文件系统。也支持从标准输入中读取输入写入目标文件系统。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -put localfile /user/hadoop/hadoopfile</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -put localfile1 localfile2 /user/hadoop/hadoopdir</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>

<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224526997"></a><a name="N102B0"></a><a name="setrep"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526997;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.21</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224526997;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">setrep</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -setrep [-R] &lt;path&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">改变一个文件的副本系数。</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">-R</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">选项用于递归改变目录下所有文件的副本系数。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>

<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527000"></a><a name="N1031B"></a><a name="test"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527000;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.24</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527000;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">test</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -test -[ezd] URI</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">选项：</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><br>-e </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">检查文件是否存在。如果存在则返回</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">0</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">-z </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">检查文件是否是</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">0</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">字节。如果是则返回</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">0</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">。</span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">-d </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">如果路径是个目录，则返回</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">1</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，否则返回</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">0</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -test -e filename</span></span></span><span style="color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527001"></a><a name="N1033E"></a><a name="text"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527001;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.25</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527001;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">text</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -text &lt;src&gt;</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">将源文件输出为文本格式。允许的格式是</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">zip</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">和</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">TextRecordInputStream</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527002"></a><a name="N10350"></a><a name="touchz"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527002;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">3.26</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>    </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527002;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">touchz</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">使用方法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop fs -touchz URI [URI …]</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">创建一个</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">0</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">字节的空文件。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">示例：</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 21pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -21pt; line-height: 12pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 21.0pt;" align="left"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-family: Wingdings; mso-fareast-font-family: Wingdings; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">n<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span class="codefrag"><span style='color: black; font-family: "Courier New"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt;' lang="EN-US">hadoop -touchz pathname</span></span></span><span style="color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">返回值：</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><br></span><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">成功返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">0</span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，失败返回</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">-1</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';">。</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="apple-style-span"><span style="color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small;"> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<h1 style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt 21.6pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 21.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527003"><span style="font-size: 15pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>         </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 15pt; color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';">命令手册</span></span></a><span style='font-size: 15pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h1>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527004"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">4.1</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>        </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-size: small;">概述</span></span></span></a></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">所有的</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">hadoop</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">命令均由</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">bin/hadoop</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">脚本引发。不指定参数运行</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">hadoop</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">脚本会打印所有命令的描述。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span class="codefrag"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New';"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">用法：</span></span></span><span class="codefrag"><span style='font-size: 10.5pt; color: black; font-family: "Courier New";' lang="EN-US">hadoop [--config confdir] [COMMAND] [GENERIC_OPTIONS] [COMMAND_OPTIONS]</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">Hadoop</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">有一个选项解析框架用于解析一般的选项和运行类。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527005"></a><a name="N10061"></a><a name="%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%84%E9%80%89%E9%A1%B9"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527005;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.1.1<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527005;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';">常规选项</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">下面的选项被</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#dfsadmin" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: #0000ff;">dfsadmin</span></a>,<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#fs" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: #0000ff;">fs</span></a>,<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#fsck" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: #0000ff;">fsck</span></a></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">和</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#job" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: #0000ff;">job</span></a></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">支持。</span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;"> </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">应用程序要实现</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.18.2/api/org/apache/hadoop/util/Tool.html" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Tool</span></a></span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">来支持</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; <h3 style="margin: 12pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: 0cm; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: none; tab-stops: 21.0pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;"> </span></span></h3>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527006"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">4.2</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>        </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-size: small;">用户命令</span></span></span></a></h2>
<p style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US">hadoop</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Verdana; mso-hansi-font-family: Verdana;">集群用户的常用命令。</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: black; font-family: Verdana;" lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527007"></a><a name="N1010C"></a><a name="archive"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527007;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.1<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527007;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">archive</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">创建一个</span><span style="color: black;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop</span></span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">档案文件。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> <span style="color: black;"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hadoop_archives.html" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: black; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">Hadoop Archives</span></a>.</span></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop archive -archiveName NAME &lt;src&gt;* &lt;dest&gt;<span style="color: black;"></span></span></span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527008"></a><a name="N10157"></a><a name="distcp"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527008;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.2<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527008;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">distcp</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">递归地拷贝文件或目录。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/distcp.html" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">DistCp</span></span><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; text-decoration: none; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; text-underline: none;" lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">指南</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">以获取等多信息。</span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527009"></a><a name="N10194"></a><a name="fs"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527009;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.3<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527009;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">fs</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop fs [</span><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%84%E9%80%89%E9%A1%B9" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">GENERIC_OPTIONS</span></span></a><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">] [COMMAND_OPTIONS]</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><span style="font-size: small;">运行一个常规的文件系统客户端。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">各种命令选项可以参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hdfs_shell.html" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">HDFS Shell</span></span><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; text-decoration: none; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; text-underline: none;" lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">指南</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。</span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527010"></a><a name="N101B0"></a><a name="fsck"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527010;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.4<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527010;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">fsck</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">运行</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">HDFS</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件系统检查工具。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hdfs_user_guide.html#fsck" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Fsck</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">了解更多。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop fsck [</span><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%84%E9%80%89%E9%A1%B9" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">GENERIC_OPTIONS</span></span></a><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">] &lt;path&gt; [-move | -delete | -openforwrite] [-files [-blocks [-locations | -racks]]]</span></span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527011"></a><a name="N10244"></a><a name="jar"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527011;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.5<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527011;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">jar</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">运行</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">jar</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件。用户可以把他们的</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Map Reduce</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">代码捆绑到</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">jar</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件中，使用这个命令执行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;">：</span><span style="mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop jar &lt;jar&gt; [mainClass] args...</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">streaming</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">作业是通过这个命令执行的。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/streaming.html#%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E4%BE%8B%E5%AD%90" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none; mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Streaming examples</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中的例子。</span><span style="mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Word count</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">例子也是通过</span><span style="mso-ansi-language: PT-BR;" lang="PT-BR"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">jar</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">命令运行的。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/mapred_tutorial.html#%E7%94%A8%E6%B3%95" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Wordcount example</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。</span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527012"></a><a name="job"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527012;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.6<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527012;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">job</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用于和</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Map Reduce</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">作业交互和命令。</span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527014"></a><a name="N103C7"></a><a name="version"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527014;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.8<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527014;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">version</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><span style="font-size: small;">打印版本信息。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop version</span></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527015"></a><a name="N103D7"></a><a name="CLASSNAME"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527015;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.2.9<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527015;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">CLASSNAME</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">脚本可用于调调用任何类。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop CLASSNAME</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">运行名字为</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">CLASSNAME</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的类。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt 28.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><a name="_Toc224527016"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">4.3</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>        </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-size: small;">管理命令</span></span></span></a></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">集群管理员常用的命令。</span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527017"></a><a name="N103F4"></a><a name="balancer"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527017;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.1<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527017;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">balancer</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">运行集群平衡工具。管理员可以简单的按</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Ctrl-C</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">来停止平衡过程。参考</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hdfs_user_guide.html#Rebalancer" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Rebalancer</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">了解更多。</span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527020"></a><a name="N1048B"></a><a name="dfsadmin"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527020;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.4<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527020;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">dfsadmin</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">运行一个<span lang="EN-US">HDFS</span>的<span lang="EN-US">dfsadmin</span>客户端。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">用法：<span lang="EN-US">hadoop dfsadmin [<span style="color: black;"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/commands_manual.html#%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%84%E9%80%89%E9%A1%B9" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: black; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">GENERIC_OPTIONS</span></a></span>] [-report] [-safemode enter | leave | get | wait] [-refreshNodes] [-finalizeUpgrade] [-upgradeProgress status | details | force] [-metasave filename] [-setQuota &lt;quota&gt; &lt;dirname&gt;...&lt;dirname&gt;] [-clrQuota &lt;dirname&gt;...&lt;dirname&gt;] [-help [cmd]]<span style="color: black;"></span></span></span></span></p>

<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-report</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">报告文件系统的基本信息和统计信息。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>

<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 2;">
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-safemode enter | leave | get | wait</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">安全模式维护命令。安全模式是</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的一个状态，这种状态下，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">1. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">不接受对名字空间的更改</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">(</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">只读</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">2. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">不复制或删除块</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">会在启动时自动进入安全模式，当配置的块最小百分比数满足最小的副本数条件时，会自动离开安全模式。安全模式可以手动进入，但是这样的话也必须手动关闭安全模式。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
