<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-refreshNodes</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">重新读取</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hosts</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">exclude</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件，更新允许连到</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的或那些需要退出或入编的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Datanode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的集合。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-finalizeUpgrade</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">终结</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">HDFS</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的升级操作。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Datanode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">删除前一个版本的工作目录，之后</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">也这样做。这个操作完结整个升级过程。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-upgradeProgress status | details | force</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">请求当前系统的升级状态，状态的细节，或者强制升级操作进行。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 6;">
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-metasave filename</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">保存</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的主要数据结构到</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop.log.dir</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">属性指定的目录下的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;filename&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件。对于下面的每一项，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;filename&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中都会一行内容与之对应</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">1. Namenode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">收到的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Datanode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的心跳信号</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">2. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">等待被复制的块</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">3. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">正在被复制的块</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">4. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">等待被删除的块</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 7;">
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-setQuota &lt;quota&gt; &lt;dirname&gt;...&lt;dirname&gt;</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">为每个目录</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> &lt;dirname&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">设定配额</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;quota&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。目录配额是一个长整型整数，强制限定了目录树下的名字个数。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">命令会在这个目录上工作良好，以下情况会报错：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">1. N</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">不是一个正整数，或者</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">2. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用户不是管理员，或者</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">3. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">这个目录不存在或是文件，或者</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">4. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">目录会马上超出新设定的配额。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 8;">
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-clrQuota &lt;dirname&gt;...&lt;dirname&gt;</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">为每一个目录</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;dirname&gt;</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">清除配额设定。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">命令会在这个目录上工作良好，以下情况会报错：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">1. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">这个目录不存在或是文件，或者</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">2. </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用户不是管理员。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">如果目录原来没有配额不会报错。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 9; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;">
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">-help [cmd]</span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">显示给定命令的帮助信息，如果没有给定命令，则显示所有命令的帮助信息。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527021"></a><a name="N1054B"></a><a name="jobtracker"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527021;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.5<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527021;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">jobtracker</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">运行<span lang="EN-US">MapReduce job Tracker</span>节点。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">用法：<span lang="EN-US">hadoop jobtracker<span style="color: black;"></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527022"></a><a name="N1055B"></a><a name="namenode"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527022;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.6<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527022;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">namenode</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">运行<span lang="EN-US">namenode</span>。有关升级，回滚，升级终结的更多信息请参考<span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hdfs_user_guide.html#%E5%8D%87%E7%BA%A7%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%9E%E6%BB%9A" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: black; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;" lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">升级和回滚</span></span></a></span>。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">用法：<span lang="EN-US">hadoop namenode [-format] | [-upgrade] | [-rollback] | [-finalize] | [-importCheckpoint]<span style="color: black;"></span></span></span></span></p>

<td style="background: white; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid; padding: 0cm;" valign="top">

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527023"></a><a name="N105C2"></a><a name="secondarynamenode"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527023;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.7<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527023;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">secondarynamenode</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">运行<span lang="EN-US">HDFS</span>的<span lang="EN-US">secondary namenode</span>。参考<span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://hadoop.apache.org/core/docs/r0.19.0/cn/hdfs_user_guide.html#Secondary+NameNode" rel="nofollow"><span style="color: black; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">Secondary Namenode</span></a></span>了解更多。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 6pt 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 0cm; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="font-size: small;">用法：<span lang="EN-US">hadoop secondarynamenode [-checkpoint [force]] | [-geteditsize]<span style="color: black;"></span></span></span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin: 13.5pt 0cm 7.8pt 36pt; layout-grid-mode: char; mso-para-margin-top: 13.5pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-line-height-alt: 12.0pt;"><a name="_Toc224527024"></a><a name="N105FF"></a><a name="tasktracker"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527024;"><span style="font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Trebuchet MS';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4.3.8<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc224527024;"><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US">tasktracker</span></span></span><span style='font-size: 13pt; color: black; font-family: "Trebuchet MS";' lang="EN-US"></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">运行</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">MapReduce</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">task Tracker</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">节点。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">用法：</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop tasktracker</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 7.8pt; layout-grid-mode: char; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<h1 style="margin: 12pt 0cm 7.8pt 18pt; layout-grid-mode: char; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-para-margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .5gd; mso-para-margin-left: 18.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Arial;">5</span><span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>          </span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">附录</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Arial;">HDFS </span></span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">测试组网方案</span></span></h1>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">一，配置策略</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">   </span></span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Hdfs</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">由</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">、</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">SecondaryNameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">DataNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">三种网元组成。各网元作用以及部署策略如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; text-indent: -18pt; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6; tab-stops: list 39.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">1，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">NameNode</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">作为</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Master</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，部署在一台机器上。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Fsimage</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">editslog</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">是系统最核心的元数据信息，为了保证元数据信息的可靠性，将</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Fsimage</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">editslog</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">在</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">SecondaryNameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">上各备份一份。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; text-indent: -18pt; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6; tab-stops: list 39.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">2，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">SecondaryNameNode</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，用来归并</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">上的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Fsimage</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">editslog</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，形成</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">checkpoint </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，同时避免</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">editslog</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">文件过大。部署在一台机器上。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; text-indent: -18pt; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6; tab-stops: list 39.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">3，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>   </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">DataNode</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">负责</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Data Block</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的读写工作，并且在</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">MapRed</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">时，作为数据源，一般和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">TaskTracker</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">部署在一起。每个</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">DataNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">占用一台机器。当需要</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">MapRed</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">时，每台机器上部署一个</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">DataNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和一个</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">TaskTracker</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">服务；</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">        </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> <img src="http://p.blog.csdn.net/images/p_blog_csdn_net/cloudeep/EntryImages/20090817/1.jpg" alt=""></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">JobTracker</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">是</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">MapRed</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中的网元，单独占用一台服务器，暂保留。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">从增强容错方面的考虑，需要定期备份</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">SecondaryNameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">上生成的</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">CheckPoint</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">根据</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hdfs</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">官方网站上的参数配置，我们的测试环境节点数较少，采用默认配置即可，可在测试过程中，根据情况进行调整。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">二，测试环境</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">   </span></span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">         </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">现有服务器如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">组</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">A</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">：</span><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.10,10.24.1.12,10.24.1.14,10.24.1.16,10.24.1.18,</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">组</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">B</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">：</span><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.24, 10.24.1.26</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">10.24.1.242</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">10.24.1.244</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">10.24.1.246</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">其中</span><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.24</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">的密码是</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">root/ mSpaCes0.2</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">外，其余均为默认密码</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop123</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">组</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">A</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中机器，</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Schubert</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">在做测试，其中</span><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.10</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">为</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Master</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，即</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">、</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">SecondaryNameNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">JobTracker</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">节点，其余为</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">DataNode</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">和</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">TaskTracker</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。采用默认端口配置。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">组</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">B</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中没有</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">环境，可用来作为</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">Master</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">节点。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="font-size: small; font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">三，节点分配</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">根据节点磁盘空间和内存使用情况，分配如下：<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; text-indent: -15pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7; tab-stops: list 45.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">1，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>       </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">选取节点 <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">RAID0-DB3</span>（<span lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span lang="EN-US">.244</span>）</strong>为<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">NameNode</span></strong>。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7; tab-stops: list 45.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">2，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>       </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">选取节点<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">demo-LVS1</span>（<span lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span lang="EN-US">.26</span>）</strong>为<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Secondary NameNode</span></strong>，并通过<span lang="EN-US">nfs</span>，共享一个目录给<span lang="EN-US">NameNode</span>作为<span lang="EN-US">FsImage</span>和<span lang="EN-US">Editslog</span>的备份目录；</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7; tab-stops: list 45.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">3，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>       </span></span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US">demo-LVS1</span></strong></span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">（<span lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span><span lang="EN-US">.26</span>）</span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">除外，<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">均为<span lang="EN-US">DataNode</span></strong>，每个节点分配存储空间约为<span lang="EN-US">700G</span>。总存储空间为<span lang="EN-US">700G</span>×<span lang="EN-US">9=6300G</span>。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">预分配内存按照<span lang="EN-US">hdfs</span>默认参数配置，通常为<span lang="EN-US">1G</span>。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">即分配表如下：<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<div>
<table class="MsoNormalTable" style="margin: auto auto auto 4.65pt; border-collapse: collapse; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-padding-alt: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt; mso-border-insideh: .5pt solid windowtext; mso-border-insidev: .5pt solid windowtext; mso-table-layout-alt: fixed;" border="1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tbody>
<tr style="height: 14.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes;">
<td style="padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; padding-bottom: 0cm; width: 108.75pt; padding-top: 0cm; height: 14.25pt; background-color: transparent; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; border: windowtext 1pt solid;" width="145" valign="bottom">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;" align="left"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">主机名<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
</td>
<td style="border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; border-top: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-left: 5.4pt; padding-bottom: 0cm; border-left: #f0f0f0; width: 81pt; padding-top: 0cm; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; height: 14.25pt; background-color: transparent; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt;" width="108" valign="bottom">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;" align="left"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">地址<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四，配置参数设置</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;"><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">系统相关参数如下：<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 60.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">1，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>                 </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">${HADOOP_HOME} </span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">目录为</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> /opt/hdfs_test/hadoop-0.19.1,</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">即</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">hadoop-0.19.1</span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">源文件放在该目下。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 60.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">2，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>                 </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">${HADOOP_HOME}/conf/hadoop-env.sh</span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">修改如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; text-indent: 12pt; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo8; tab-stops: list 42.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">a)<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>  </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">设置</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">JAVA_HOME</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">环境变量：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">export JAVA_HOME=/usr/local/j2sdk</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; text-indent: 12pt; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo8; tab-stops: list 42.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">b)<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'> </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">设置</span><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">HADOOP_PID_DIR</span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">环境变量：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt; text-indent: 21pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">export HADOOP_PID_DIR=${HADOOP_HOME}/run/pids</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 60.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">3，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>                 </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">${HADOOP_HOME}/conf/masters</span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中添加</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">secondary namenode</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">地址如下：、</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.26</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 60.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">4，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>                 </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">${HADOOP_HOME}/conf/slaves</span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">中添加</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">datanode</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">地址列表如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.10</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.12</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.14</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.16</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.18</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.24</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.242</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.244</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 105pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">10.24.1</span></strong><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">.246</span></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60pt; text-indent: -39pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 60.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">5，<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>                 </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">${HADOOP_HOME}/conf/hadoop-site.xml</span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">修改如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; text-indent: 12pt; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo8; tab-stops: list 42.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">a)<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>  </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">添加参数</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">hadoop.tmp.dir</span></strong></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;property&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;name&gt;<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">hadoop.tmp.dir</strong>&lt;/name&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;value&gt;<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">/data/hdfs_test/ hadoop-${user.name}</strong>&lt;/value&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;description&gt;A base for other temporary directories.&lt;/description&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;/property&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; text-indent: 12pt; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo8; tab-stops: list 42.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">b)<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'> </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">添加参数</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"> <span lang="EN-US">fs.default.name</span></span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，即</span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">NameNodeURI</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">。<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">相关端口在默认值基础上增加</strong></span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">1000</span></span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">，其余端口亦按此规则修改。</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;property&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;name&gt;<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">fs.default.name</strong>&lt;/name&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;value&gt;<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">hdfs://</strong></span></span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;" lang="EN-US">RAID0-DB3</span></strong><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">:10000</span></strong><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US">&lt;/value&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;description&gt;The name of the default file system.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>A URI whose</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>scheme and authority determine the FileSystem implementation.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>The</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>uri's scheme determines the config property (fs.SCHEME.impl) naming</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>the FileSystem implementation class.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>The uri's authority is used to</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>determine the host, port, etc. for a filesystem.&lt;/description&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;">&lt;/property&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; text-indent: 12pt; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo8; tab-stops: list 42.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman';" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">c)<span style='font: 7pt "Times New Roman";'>  </span></span></span><span dir="ltr"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Secondary namenode,datanode,namenode</strong></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 9pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman';">相关<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">端口</strong>配置如下：</span><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">      </span>of directories then the transaction file is replicated in all of the </span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;value&gt;<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">${hadoop.tmp.dir}/name_checkpoint/local,${hadoop.tmp.dir}/ name_checkpoint /bak1</strong>&lt;/value&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>&lt;description&gt;Determines where on the local filesystem the DFS secondary</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">      </span>name node should store the temporary images to merge.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt;"><span style="font-size: 9pt;" lang="EN-US"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">      </span>If this is a comma-delimited list of directories then the image is</span></span></p>
